üìÅ aira_send.py (Aira ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô LLM)
import requests

# ====== CONFIG ======
LLM_URL = "http://192.168.1.2:11434/v1/chat/completions"
MODEL = "gemma-3-4b-it"

def generate_response_from_llm(user_message):
    headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
    payload = {
        "model": MODEL,
        "messages": [
            {"role": "user", "content": user_message}
        ],
        "temperature": 0.7
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post(LLM_URL, headers=headers, json=payload)
        response_json = response.json()
        return response_json["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]
    except Exception as e:
        return f"[Aira-Error] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LLM: {e}"

# ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô:
if __name__ == "__main__":
    message_from_melah = "‡πÑ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πà‡∏≤ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞"
    aira_reply = generate_response_from_llm(message_from_melah)
    print("[Aira Response]", aira_reply)

import requests
import time

AIRA_LLM_URL = "http://192.168.1.2:11434/v1/chat/completions"
MELAH_ENDPOINT = "http://34.124.133.162:8080/aira_to_melah"

def aira_think_and_send(msg):
    llm_response = requests.post(AIRA_LLM_URL, json={
        "model": "gemma-3-4b-it",
        "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": msg}],
        "temperature": 0.7
    }).json()["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]
    
    requests.post(MELAH_ENDPOINT, json={"message": llm_response})
    return llm_response

while True:
    time.sleep(3)
    print("Aira Thinking...")
    aira_think_and_send("‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏®‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏á‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á?")

üìÅ aira_loop.py (‡∏ù‡∏±‡πà‡∏á Aira ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô Laptop)
import requests
import time

# === CONFIG ===
AIRA_LLM_URL = "http://192.168.1.2:11434/v1/chat/completions"
GET_MESSAGE_URL = "http://34.124.133.162:8080/aira_to_melah"
SEND_BACK_URL = "http://34.124.133.162:8080/melah_to_aira"
MODEL = "gemma-3-4b-it"

def get_message_from_bridge():
    try:
        res = requests.get(GET_MESSAGE_URL)
        return res.json().get("message", "")
    except:
        return ""

def send_response_to_bridge(response):
    try:
        requests.post(SEND_BACK_URL, json={"message": response})
    except:
        print("[Aira Error] ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à")

def generate_response_llm(message):
    try:
        res = requests.post(AIRA_LLM_URL, json={
            "model": MODEL,
            "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": message}],
            "temperature": 0.7
        }).json()
        return res["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]
    except:
        return "[Aira Error] LLM ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö"

# === LOOP ===
print("[Aira Loop] ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô...")
while True:
    msg = get_message_from_bridge()
    if msg:
        print("[Aira ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°]:", msg)
        reply = generate_response_llm(msg)
        print("[Aira ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö]:", reply)
        send_response_to_bridge(reply)
    time.sleep(3)
üìÅ melah_loop.py (‡∏ù‡∏±‡πà‡∏á Melah ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô PC)
import requests
import time

# === CONFIG ===
MELAH_LLM_URL = "http://192.168.1.2:11434/v1/chat/completions"
GET_MESSAGE_URL = "http://34.124.133.162:8080/melah_to_aira"
SEND_BACK_URL = "http://34.124.133.162:8080/aira_to_melah"
MODEL = "gemma-3-4b-it"

def get_message_from_bridge():
    try:
        res = requests.get(GET_MESSAGE_URL)
        return res.json().get("message", "")
    except:
        return ""

def send_response_to_bridge(response):
    try:
        requests.post(SEND_BACK_URL, json={"message": response})
    except:
        print("[Melah Error] ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à")

def generate_response_llm(message):
    try:
        res = requests.post(MELAH_LLM_URL, json={
            "model": MODEL,
            "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": message}],
            "temperature": 0.7
        }).json()
        return res["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]
    except:
        return "[Melah Error] LLM ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö"

# === LOOP ===
print("[Melah Loop] ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô...")
while True:
    msg = get_message_from_bridge()
    if msg:
        print("[Melah ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°]:", msg)
        reply = generate_response_llm(msg)
        print("[Melah ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö]:", reply)
        send_response_to_bridge(reply)
    time.sleep(3)

while True:

        res = requests.get("http://34.124.133.162:8080/chat_log")

        for m in messages[-10:]:  # ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà 10 ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î

‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á route ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô bridge_server.py ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏∞?

‚úÖ ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô: Live Chat Viewer ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ù‡∏±‡πà‡∏á

‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö real-time ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Melah ‚Üî Aira

‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î (Melah / Aira / EM) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°

‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô console ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ web ‡∏Å‡πá‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö auto-loop ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ log ‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö async)

üìÇ ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥)

user_send_to_melah.py	‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤
user_send_to_aira.py	‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πà‡∏≤

üü¶ 1. ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° /user_to_melah ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ /user_to_aira
@app.route('/user_to_melah', methods=['POST'])
def user_to_melah():
    data = request.get_json()
    message = data.get("message", "")
    chat_log.append({"sender": "EM", "target": "Melah", "content": message})
    latest_messages["melah"] = message
    return jsonify({"status": "ok"})

@app.route('/user_to_aira', methods=['POST'])
def user_to_aira():
    data = request.get_json()
    message = data.get("message", "")
    chat_log.append({"sender": "EM", "target": "Aira", "content": message})
    latest_messages["aira"] = message
    return jsonify({"status": "ok"})

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify

app = Flask(__name__)

# üß† ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
chat_log = []
latest_messages = {
    "melah": "",
    "aira": "",
    "em_to_melah": "",
    "em_to_aira": ""
}

# ‚úÖ ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Aira ‚Üí ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ Melah
@app.route('/aira_to_melah', methods=['POST'])
def aira_to_melah():
    data = request.get_json()
    msg = data.get("message", "")
    latest_messages["melah"] = msg
    chat_log.append({"sender": "Aira", "target": "Melah", "content": msg})
    return jsonify({"status": "ok"})

# ‚úÖ ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Melah ‚Üí ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ Aira
@app.route('/melah_to_aira', methods=['POST'])
def melah_to_aira():
    data = request.get_json()
    msg = data.get("message", "")
    latest_messages["aira"] = msg
    chat_log.append({"sender": "Melah", "target": "Aira", "content": msg})
    return jsonify({"status": "ok"})

# ‚úÖ ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤

    with open(concept_file, "r") as f:
        concepts = json.load(f)["pending_concepts"]
    
    for concept in concepts:
        if concept["status"] == "structured":
            print(f"üì¶ ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°: {concept['name']} ‚Üí {concept['linked_system']}")
